<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column82846_4ab732-53"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id82846_a2c65f-95 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

	<article class="entry content-bg loop-entry post-90127 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-soup category-high-protein tag-comfort-food tag-gluten-free tag-lazy-vegan tag-meal-prep tag-reader-favorites tag-root-veggies tag-tree-nut-free">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column82846_9605e8-ed"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h2 class="kt-adv-heading82846_a83342-fe wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading82846_a83342-fe">Hi, I&#8217;m Kim-Julie!</h2>



<p>Before going vegan (somewhat accidentally and overnight) in 2011, I was the furthest thing from a vegan you could possibly imagine. I LOVED meat, fish, eggs, cheese, and honey. That’s why I know how overwhelming it can seem to change your lifestyle and eating habits. On&nbsp;this blog, I teach you how to do it one step at a time, with lots of delicious, quick and easy recipes.&nbsp;</p>
